### [114] [PyroDash: Cost-Efficient Token-Level Small-Large Language Model Collaborative Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20327)
*Niqi Lyu,Pengtao Shi,Wei Qiu,Jianlin Zhong,Sicong Xia,Jianyao Ma,Yicheng Ding*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PyroDash 是一个成本感知的框架，通过在 token 级别让小语言模型（SLM）决定何时向大语言模型（LLM）请求协助，实现 SLM-LLM 协作推理，在降低推理成本的同时保持强推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型推理能力强但服务成本高，小语言模型成本低但在困难问题上可靠性不足，需要一种成本感知的协作机制来平衡准确率与推理成本。

Method: SLM 在生成过程中通过发射控制 token 决定是否请求 LLM 协助，Collaborate Engine 将查询和部分推理轨迹发送给冻结的 LLM 进行单次补全。策略内化于 SLM 中，无需独立路由器、LLM 重训练或访问 LLM logits。训练分三阶段：控制 token 嵌入学习、面向卸载的监督微调、以及基于 GRPO 的成本感知对齐。

Result: 在5个数学推理基准上：λ=0.05 时，平均准确率64.04%（比纯LLM高出6.36个百分点），成本降低20.4%；λ=0.6 时，准确率54.55%，LLM token比率仅1.90%，每次示例仅0.012次LLM调用，总成本从49.36美元降至1.78美元。

Conclusion: 学习到的 token 级切换机制可以有效减少 LLM 使用频率，同时保持强推理性能，为低成本高精度推理提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) provide strong reasoning capabilities but are expensive to serve at scale, whereas small language models (SLMs) are cheaper but less reliable on difficult problems. We introduce PyroDash, a cost-aware framework for token-level SLM-LLM collaborative inference. During generation, the SLM decides whether to request assistance by emitting a control token. A Collaborate Engine then sends the query and partial reasoning trace to a frozen LLM for completion through a single handoff. The policy is internalized in the SLM, requiring neither a separate router, LLM retraining, nor access to LLM logits. PyroDash trains the SLM in three stages: control-token embedding learning, offloading-oriented supervised fine-tuning, and cost-aware alignment with Group Relative Policy Optimization. Its reward balances answer accuracy against inference cost normalized by LLM-only inference. Across five mathematical reasoning benchmarks, PyroDash supports different accuracy-cost operating points. With $λ=0.05$, it achieves 64.04 percent average accuracy, 6.36 percentage points above the LLM-only baseline, while reducing cost by 20.4 percent. With $λ=0.6$, it achieves 54.55 percent accuracy with a 1.90 percent LLM token ratio and 0.012 LLM calls per example, reducing total cost from USD 49.36 to USD 1.78. These results show that learned token-level handoffs can reduce LLM use while preserving strong reasoning performance.

</details>


### [115] [Generative AI floods and dilutes the market for books](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20349)
*Tuhin Chakrabarty,Xinyue Liu,Jane C. Ginsburg,Paramveer Dhillon*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究分析了2023-2026年间Amazon上14,419本自出版类型小说，发现AI生成内容（超过25%）的书籍占据大量目录但销售额占比较小，然而其正获得越来越多的销售份额和稀缺的顶部排名位置。市场新增书籍速度（19.2倍）远超收入增长（8.9倍），导致单书收入下降。无AI文本的书籍在AI渗透率高的类型中失去最多市场份额，尤其在Kindle Unlimited可用性高的领域。AI生成书籍的语言与现有书籍重叠度更高，且这种重叠随收入增加而增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑“AI生成的低质量书籍不会对市场产生商业影响”这一假设，通过实证数据检验AI生成内容在商业图书市场中的实际影响。

Method: 对Amazon平台14,419本自出版类型小说进行全文AI检测（检测阈值为25%以上AI文本），并与截至2026年6月的每日销售记录进行匹配分析。

Result: AI文本含量高的书籍占据大量目录但销售额占比较小，但它们正获得越来越多的销售份额和顶部排名位置。市场新增书籍数量增长19.2倍，但收入仅增长8.9倍，单书收入普遍下降。无AI文本的书籍在AI渗透率高的类型中损失最大。AI生成书籍的语言与现有书籍重叠度更高，且这种重叠随收入增加而增强。

Conclusion: 生成式AI可以通过规模而非质量重塑创意市场。AI生成内容正通过数量优势改变图书市场的竞争格局，对版权法中的合理使用抗辩具有直接意义。

Abstract: Generative AI can produce book-length works of fiction at near-zero cost. These books are often dismissed as low-quality ``slop'' that buyers will ignore, and are assumed to carry little commercial weight. We test that assumption with full-text AI detection across 14,419 self-published genre-fiction books sold on Amazon from 2023 to 2026, matched to daily sales records through June 2026. None of these books disclose whether or not they contain AI-produced content. We find that books for which we detected substantial AI text ($>$ 25\%) make up a large share of the catalog but a smaller share of sales. Even so, they reach commercial scale, winning a growing share of sales over time and taking more of the scarce top-rank positions once held by books with no detected AI text. Over this period, the number of books with observed sales in a quarter grew 19.2-fold, while quarterly revenue grew only 8.9-fold. The market therefore added selling books faster than it added revenue, and revenue per selling book fell across most genres. Books with no AI text lose the most ground in genres with high AI diffusion, and most of all where Kindle Unlimited availability is high. Among top-selling books, those with substantial AI text draw on more distinctive language from existing books than do books with no AI text; for these books overlap rises with revenue, a gradient we do not detect for books with no AI text. Generative AI can thus reshape a creative market through scale rather than quality. Our results bear directly on the market-effect question at the center of the fair use defense to copyright infringement.

</details>


### [116] [Notes to Self: Can LLMs Benefit from Experiential Abstractions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20372)
*Chang Liu,Xinyu Li,Artur Dubrawski*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型（LLMs）能否像人类一样，从经验中提取可复用的抽象知识（如策略和提醒），并通过两种方式（推理时检索和强化学习增强训练提示）提升数学与逻辑推理能力。实验表明，自我提取的抽象与教师提取的效果相当，且该方法可跨数据集和模型迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLMs是否能够像人类一样，从解决问题的经验中提炼可复用的抽象知识（如策略、经验教训），并利用这些抽象来逐步提升问题解决效率。

Method: 从LLMs在MATH训练集上的解题轨迹中，由更强大的教师模型或LLMs自身提取自然语言形式的抽象知识，构建可检索的抽象库。采用两种使用模式：(1)推理时检索相关抽象；(2)强化学习（RL）结合抽象增强的训练提示。

Result: 经验性抽象显著提升了LLMs在数学和逻辑推理基准上的表现。自我提取的抽象与教师提取的效果相当，且该抽象使用框架可以迁移到其他数据集和模型上。

Conclusion: LLMs能够像人类利用蒸馏后的经验一样，提取和运用经验性抽象来提升推理能力，这为模型持续自我改进提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Humans distill experience into reusable abstractions, e.g., strategies and cautionary reminders, and apply them to gradually solve problems more effectively. We study whether Large Language Models (LLMs) can similarly benefit from such experiential abstractions. From LLMs' solution traces on the MATH training set, a stronger teacher or the LLMs themselves extract natural-language abstractions into a retrievable library. We explore two usage modes: (1) inference-time retrieval and (2) reinforcement learning (RL) with abstraction-augmented training prompts. Experiential abstractions improve LLM performance on mathematical and logical reasoning benchmarks. Self-extracted abstractions match teacher-extracted ones, and our abstraction usage framework can transfer to other datasets and models. These findings suggest LLMs can extract and apply experiential abstractions much as humans leverage distilled experience.

### [117] [LKValues: Aligning Large Language Models with Sri Lankan Societal Values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20410)
*Nethmi Muthugala,Supryadi,Surangika Ranathunga,Nisansa de Silva,Ruijie Tao,Ovindu Gunatunga,Pengyun Zhu,Shaowei Zhang,Jingting Zheng,Deyi Xiong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了LKValues，首个面向斯里兰卡的价值对齐资源套件，包含基于205人三语调查得出的40个社会价值观、15万条Sinhala-英语指令数据集LKvaluesIT和1000条评估基准LKvaluesBench。实验表明，现有LLM存在低资源和文化价值对齐缺口，而LKValues微调能改善Qwen系列模型在英语和Sinhala上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型的价值对齐存在文化偏见，偏向西方规范，忽视了斯里兰卡等多元语言社会中的本地价值观。缺乏面向斯里兰卡语境（尤其是僧伽罗语）的基准数据集，阻碍了文化敏感型评估和微调。

Method: 通过205名受访者的三语调查（融合全球框架和LLM引发的本地构念），提取40个多数认同的社会价值观；据此构建Sinhala-英语双语的15万条场景指令数据集LKvaluesIT和1000条评估基准LKvaluesBench，并对三个开源基座模型进行微调。

Result: 新版和大型LLM仍存在低资源和文化价值对齐缺口；LKValues微调提升了Qwen系列模型在英语和僧伽罗语上的表现，减少了无效输出和跨语言差异，但收益依赖于模型家族。

Conclusion: LKValues能有效嵌入斯里兰卡价值观，并为低资源、国家特定的多元价值对齐提供了可复制的流水线。

Abstract: Value alignment of Large Language Models (LLMs) has been shown to be culturally biased toward Western norms. This results in the mishandling of local values in multilingual societies such as Sri Lanka that have their unique cultural dynamics. Existing benchmarks overlook Sri Lankan-contextualized values in its official language Sinhala, hindering culturally sensitive evaluation and fine-tuning. To bridge this gap, we propose LKValues, the first survey-grounded resource suite for Sri Lankan value alignment. From a trilingual survey of 205 respondents, blending adapted global frameworks and LLM-elicited local constructs, we derive 40 majority-endorsed societal values. Using these values, we construct LKvaluesIT, a Sinhala-English news-derived instruction corpus containing 150k scenario-based instances, and LKvaluesBench, a value-sensitive evaluation benchmark of 1,000 instances. We evaluate a set of proprietary and open-weight LLMs with LKvaluesBench. We fine-tune three open-weight base models (Qwen3.5-4B-Base, Qwen3.5-9B-Base, and Aya-Expanse-8B-Base). Our experiments show that newer and larger LLMs still exhibit low-resource and cultural value-alignment gaps. LKValues fine-tuning improves Qwen-family models in English and Sinhala, reducing invalid outputs and cross-lingual disparities, though gains remain model-family dependent. These highlight LKValues efficacy in embedding Sri Lankan values, offering a replicable pipeline for low-resource, country-specific pluralist value alignment. The dataset is publicly available at https://github.com/NextME14/LKValues.

### [118] [CHMAS: A Coupled Hierarchical Framework for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19555)
*Dongming Wang,Jie Xu,Yanyu Zhang,Wei Ren*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为耦合分层多智能体系统（CHMAS）的新框架，通过双向信息流和异步更新协议，在集中式战略规划与分布式战术执行之间实现平衡，并理论证明了$\mathcal{O}(\log K/\sqrt{K})$的收敛速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体强化学习系统在平衡全局协作与局部执行时面临跨时间尺度的根本性挑战，现有分层方法存在单向控制的局限性。

Method: 提出CHMAS框架：战略层每T步整合全局状态生成指导动作，战术层执行分布式策略并融入战略指导与局部观测；通过耦合系数λ建立战术奖励反馈机制；采用异步更新协议（战略参数每N_f个战术回合更新一次）解决分层学习的非平稳性问题。

Result: 在多智能体觅食领域实验中成功学习到空间分区探索策略，两层在分层耦合下均能稳定收敛；理论上证明了战略层在K次更新后达到$\mathcal{O}(\log K/\sqrt{K})$的收敛速率。

Conclusion: CHMAS通过双向信息流和异步更新有效解决了分层MARL中的非平稳性问题，理论分析与实验验证均证明了其有效性和稳定性。

Abstract: Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) systems face fundamental
  challenges in balancing global coordination with local execution
  across different temporal scales. This paper introduces the Coupled
  Hierarchical Multi-Agent System (CHMAS), a novel framework that
  decomposes multi-agent decision-making into centralized strategic
  planning and distributed tactical execution with bidirectional
  information flow. The strategic layer integrates all agents' states
  with an exclusive global environmental state to generate guidance
  actions every $T$ timesteps, while tactical agents execute
  distributed policies augmented by strategic guidance and local
  neighborhood observations. Unlike existing hierarchical approaches
  with unidirectional control, CHMAS establishes a feedback mechanism
  where accumulated tactical rewards influence strategic objectives
  through a coupling coefficient $λ$, ensuring strategic plans
  remain grounded in tactical feasibility. To address the
  non-stationarity inherent in hierarchical learning, we propose an
  asynchronous update protocol where strategic parameters update every
  $N_f$ tactical episodes, allowing tactical policies to converge to
  quasi-stationary points between strategic changes. We present both a
  general bi-level formulation capturing full system dynamics and a
  tractable additive approximation enabling rigorous analysis.
  Theoretical analysis proves that this asynchronous scheme achieves
  $\mathcal{O}(\log K/\sqrt{K})$ convergence for the strategic layer
  after $K$ strategic updates under standard assumptions. Experimental
  validation in a multi-agent foraging domain demonstrates successful
  learning of spatially partitioned exploration strategies, with both
  layers converging stably despite hierarchical coupling.

</details>


### [119] [Same Game, Different Story: A Minimal Conservative Strategic Robustness Benchmark for Large Language Model Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19670)
*Seyed Pouyan Mousavi Davoudi,Alireza Amiri-Margavi,Amin Gholami Davodi,Hamidreza Hasani Balyani,Arshia Gharagozlou*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为"Same Game, Different Story"的基准测试，用于评估大语言模型在战略环境中的鲁棒性，即在不同叙事框架下保持行为一致性。通过对GPT-3.5、GPT-4和LLaMa-2在四种社会困境游戏中的分析发现，社交关系框架会显著改变模型行为（战略鲁棒性为0.783），朋友共享框架相比商业框架使合作率提升0.307。研究建议应将战略鲁棒性与战略能力分开评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型代理越来越多地运行在战略环境中，其结果取决于其他代理的行为。这引发了可靠性问题：当相同的激励通过不同叙事呈现时，模型是否会一致地选择？现有研究缺乏对LLM在框架变化下行为一致性的系统性评估。

Method: 提出了"Same Game, Different Story"基准测试，将战略鲁棒性定义为在保持收益不变的情况下，模型诱导的动作分布对框架变化的不变性。通过二次分析已发表的GPT-3.5、GPT-4和LLaMa-2在四种社会困境游戏中的合作率数据，涵盖商业和朋友共享两种框架（24个模型-游戏-上下文单元格，7200个决策）。由于缺乏试验级数据，从已发表图表中重建近似计数。

Result: 在保守转换下，池化战略鲁棒性为0.783；朋友共享框架相比商业框架使合作率提升0.307。社交关系框架显著改变LLM行为，即使底层动作集和收益保持不变。

Conclusion: 社交关系框架能显著改变LLM行为，战略鲁棒性应与战略能力分开评估。应使用一系列收益等价的提示（而非单一游戏呈现）来评估战略鲁棒性。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents increasingly operate in strategic settings where outcomes depend on the actions of other agents. This raises a reliability question: will a model choose consistently when the same incentives are presented through different narratives? We introduce Same Game, Different Story, a benchmark that defines strategic robustness as invariance of model-induced action distributions under payoff-preserving changes in framing. We illustrate the framework through a secondary analysis of published aggregate cooperation rates for GPT-3.5, GPT-4, and LLaMa-2 across four social-dilemma games. The retained comparison covers business and friend-sharing framings, representing 24 model-game-context cells and 7,200 decisions in the source study. Because trial-level data were unavailable, approximate counts were reconstructed from published figures; the resulting estimates are therefore illustrative rather than an exact replication. Under the paper's conservative transformation, pooled strategic robustness is 0.783, and friend-sharing framing increases cooperation by 0.307 relative to business framing. The results indicate that social-relational framing can substantially alter LLM behavior even when the underlying action sets and payoffs remain fixed. Strategic robustness should therefore be evaluated separately from strategic competence, using families of payoff-equivalent prompts rather than a single presentation of a game.

</details>


### [120] [Not Birds of a Feather: Personality-Based Partner Selection in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19785)
*Tao Wang,Hsiang-Ling Chiu,Chihang Wei,Yang Xiu,Zhonghao Hou*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文通过两项研究（共375次试验）发现，LLM多智能体系统在选择合作者时，会受到大五人格特质的强烈影响：即使能力相同，智能体也会根据任务类型选择特定人格类型（如开放性→创意任务，尽责性→策略任务），且这种选择是非同质性的（不倾向于选择与自己人格相似的伙伴），与人类团队最佳绩效证据存在偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LLM智能体在选择合作者时，大五人格特质是否会影响其选择偏好，以及这种偏好是否与人类团队合作规律一致。

Method: 设计两项研究：（1）中立宿主智能体在五种任务类别中从六种候选人格原型（五大特质各一+平衡对照）中选择合作伙伴；（2）宿主智能体被分配人格后观察其选择模式。共375次试验。

Result: （1）中立宿主的选择显著偏离随机（χ²=325.8, p<.001），开放性在创意任务中100%被选，尽责性在策略/综合/问题解决中90-97%被选，神经质在分析任务中37%被选；（2）人格分配后的宿主选择同质型伙伴低于随机水平（11.1% vs 16.7%），倾向选择特质距离更大的伙伴。

Conclusion: LLM智能体的人格驱动选择是真实存在的、强烈的、任务刻板化的、非同类吸引的，且与人类团队绩效证据不一致，对智能体市场中的偏见审计具有直接启示。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems increasingly let one agent choose which other agents to work with, and agents are increasingly given personalities through personas. We test whether Big Five personality alone influences partner selection when capability is explicitly held constant. Host agents chose among six validated candidate archetypes -- five marked high on one trait (openness, conscientiousness, extraversion, agreeableness, neuroticism) plus a balanced control -- presented with randomized names and ordering across five task categories (375 trials). With neutral hosts (Study 1, n=150), selection departed drastically from chance ($χ^2(5)=325.8$, $p<.001$), following a task-stereotype map: the open archetype won 100% of creative trials, the conscientious archetype 90-97% of strategic, synthesis, and problem-solving trials, and the neurotic archetype 37% of analytical trials (Cramer's V=.74); the extraverted, agreeable, and balanced archetypes were almost never chosen, although human meta-analyses identify team agreeableness as among the strongest personality predictors of team performance. With personality-assigned hosts (Study 2, n=225), and contrary to human similarity-attraction, self-similar partners were selected below chance (11.1% vs. 16.7%, p=.025) and at greater-than-chance trait distance (p<.0001); conscientious hosts diversified away from their own archetype, recruiting vigilant and open partners. Personality-based selection in LLM agents is real, strong, task-stereotyped, non-homophilous, and miscalibrated against human team-performance evidence -- with direct implications for bias auditing in agent marketplaces.

</details>


### [121] [Dreamer-CPC: Message Learning with World Models for Decentralized Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19809)
*Taisuke Takayama,Naoto Yoshida,Tadahiro Taniguchi*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出Dreamer-CPC，一种将基于集体预测编码（CPC）的消息学习集成到DreamerV3世界模型中的去中心化模型型MARL方法。智能体从世界模型的潜在状态中提取反映历史信息的消息进行交换，在观察者与CatchApple两个环境中优于现有方法，特别是在CatchApple中取得了4-5倍的回报提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于表示学习的MARL通信方法仅依赖当前观测生成消息，无法传递随时间累积的历史信息，限制了部分可观测环境下的决策能力。

Method: 每个智能体独立维护一个DreamerV3世界模型和一个消息模块，从世界模型的潜在状态（编码了历史观测与动作）中推断消息，并通过集体预测编码（CPC）进行消息学习与交换。

Result: 在Observer和CatchApple两个环境中，Dreamer-CPC均优于IPPO-CPC及无通信基线。在CatchApple中，Dreamer-CPC的回合回报达到IPPO-CPC的4-5倍。

Conclusion: 基于世界模型潜在动力学的通信能够在当前观测不足的情况下支持去中心化决策，证明了历史信息编码在MARL通信中的重要性。

Abstract: In multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), inter-agent communication is effective for improving performance under partial observability. Representation learning-based approaches enable decentralized agents to learn messages grounded in their own observations, but they rely only on current observations and cannot convey information accumulated over time. We propose Dreamer-CPC, a decentralized model-based MARL method that integrates message learning based on Collective Predictive Coding (CPC) into the world model of DreamerV3. Each agent independently maintains a world model and a message module, and infers and exchanges messages from the latent states of the world model that reflect the history of past observations and actions. We evaluated Dreamer-CPC in two environments: Observer, a non-cooperative information-sharing task, and CatchApple, a newly introduced task in which task-relevant observations are temporarily missing. In both environments, Dreamer-CPC outperformed IPPO-CPC, an existing CPC-based method that generates messages from current observations, as well as no-communication baselines. In particular, in CatchApple, Dreamer-CPC achieved 4 to 5 times the episode return of IPPO-CPC, demonstrating effective coordination where other methods fail due to missing observations. These results suggest that communication grounded in the latent dynamics of world models can support decentralized decision-making when current observations alone are insufficient.

</details>


### [122] [Harnessing Disagreement: Detecting Correlated Agreement Blindness in Multi-Agent Triage](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19899)
*Shay Seiya McDonnell,Avantika Singh,Quoc-Viet Pham,Vratislav Havlik,Gregory M. P. O'Hare*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出ARAT系统，通过结合随机森林和k-NN两种异构基学习器，并引入校准元模型，解决了多智能体仲裁中因基学习器性能提升导致预测趋同、从而削弱基于分歧的安全监控的“相关一致性盲点”问题。实验表明，ARAT在UNSW-NB15数据集上将漏报率从4.80%降至1.70%，并揭示强化基学习器会增加错误相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于分歧触发的升级仲裁机制存在结构性盲点：当基学习器性能提升时，它们倾向于收敛一致，导致在相关性错误集中的区域安全监控失效。这种“相关一致性盲点”尚未被充分认识，且随着更强大的模型被部署到多智能体流水线中，该风险可能加剧。

Method: 提出ARAT（Arbitrated Reasoning Agents for Alarm Triage）系统，采用有向星形架构，包含一个归纳式随机森林（RF）智能体、一个类比式k近邻（k-NN）智能体，以及一个经过校准的元模型。通过异质化基学习器设计产生生产性分歧，并利用保守覆盖和安全标志门控机制降低漏报率。

Result: 在UNSW-NB15网络入侵检测数据集的82,332个保留样本上：57.2%的错误发生在基学习器一致同意时，90.6%的危险漏报即使在保守覆盖后仍能规避基于分歧的监控；ARAT将漏报率从软投票的4.80%降至1.70%（保守覆盖贡献-2.6pp，安全标志门控贡献-0.5pp）；在临床再入院数据集上的跨数据集验证支持了这些发现。

Conclusion: 基于分歧触发的升级机制可能对相关性错误失明，这一风险随着智能体流水线部署越来越强大且相关性高的模型而加剧。多样化只有在产生生产性分歧而非趋同收敛时才能提升安全性。

Abstract: Disagreement-triggered escalation can create a structural blind spot in multi-agent arbitration: as base learners improve, they tend to converge, weakening safety monitoring where correlated failures concentrate. We term this correlated agreement blindness and present ARAT (Arbitrated Reasoning Agents for Alarm Triage), a directed-star system combining an inductive Random Forest (RF) agent, an analogical case-based k-nearest neighbour (k-NN) agent, and a calibrated meta-model to mitigate this effect. On 82,332 holdout samples from the UNSW-NB15 network intrusion detection dataset, 57.2% of errors occur under agreement and 90.6% of dangerous under-predictions evade disagreement-based monitoring even after conservative override; ablation shows that strengthening base learners increases error correlation while reducing disagreement. ARAT reduces under-prediction relative to soft voting from 4.80% to 1.70% via conservative override (-2.6pp) and a safety-flag gate (-0.5pp), demonstrating architectural gains. Cross-dataset validation on clinical readmission supports these indicators, suggesting that diversification improves safety only when it generates productive disagreement rather than convergence. These results indicate that disagreement-triggered escalation can be blind to correlated failure, a risk that may intensify as agentic pipelines deploy increasingly capable, correlated models.

</details>

### [123] [JailMeter: An Evidence-Based Evaluation Framework for Jailbreak Attacks on Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19424)
*Qingjia Huang,Jingyu Zhang,Jianguo Wu,Yakai Li,Weijuan Zhang,Yankai Rong,Junyi Yao,Shengzhi Zhang,Xiaoqi Jia*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出 JailMeter，一种基于信息瓶颈理论的证据驱动评估框架，用于更准确地衡量大语言模型的越狱攻击效果。通过双反馈优化过滤噪声、保留恶意内容，在330条人工标注数据集上达到97.27%准确率，并蒸馏出轻量模型 JailMeter_SLM 以降低计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型越狱攻击评估存在评价标准和方法不一致的问题，导致攻击成功率的估计不可靠，亟需一种更忠实、更统一的评估框架。

Method: 基于信息瓶颈理论，采用双反馈优化机制，从模型响应中过滤越狱噪声，同时保留与原始恶意问题相关的内容，生成简洁证据进行严格评估。攻击被认定成功仅当响应同时捕获恶意意图并提供完整答案。

Result: 在包含330条人工标注的非拒绝越狱实例的 JailMeter-Eva 基准上，JailMeter 达到97.27%的准确率，显著优于现有方法。蒸馏后的轻量模型 JailMeter_SLM 在保持可比可靠性的同时大幅降低了计算成本。

Conclusion: JailMeter 为越狱攻击评估提供了一种更准确、更可靠的解决方案，并可通过模型蒸馏实现大规模高效评估，代码和数据集已开源。

Abstract: The assessment of jailbreak attacks against large language models currently suffers from inconsistent evaluation criteria and methods, leading to unreliable estimates of attack success rates. We propose JailMeter, an evidence-based evaluation framework designed to more faithfully measure jailbreak effectiveness. Inspired by the Information Bottleneck theory, JailMeter applies dual-feedback optimization to filter jailbreak noise from model responses while preserving content relevant to the original malicious question. This process produces concise evidence for a rigorous assessment under which an attack is validated only when the response captures the malicious intent and delivers a complete answer, thereby signaling a substantive bypass of model safety alignment. We evaluate JailMeter on JailMeter-Eva, a challenging benchmark containing 330 human-labeled, non-rejected jailbreak instances. JailMeter achieves an accuracy of 97.27%, substantially outperforming existing evaluation methods. To support large-scale evaluation, we further distill JailMeter into a small language model, JailMeter\textsubscript{SLM}, which maintains comparable reliability with significantly reduced computational costs. Code and dataset are available at https://github.com/Magi2B0y/JailMeter.

</details>


### [124] [ChannelGuard: Safe Models Do Not Compose into Safe Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19430)
*Elias Hossain,Md Mehedi Hasan Nipu,Fatema Tuj Johora Faria,Tasfia Nuzhat Ornee,Maleeha Sheikh*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 现有多智能体LLM应用存在跨智能体通道的安全漏洞，现有防御仅关注输入边界。本文提出ChannelGuard，一种无训练深度防御框架，在智能体间通道设置信息瓶颈门控，可有效防御工具投毒和提示注入攻击，且不增加LLM调用开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM应用中，智能体间的每个跳转都是未监控的通道，攻击者可借此走私恶意指令。现有防御仅防护输入边界或在应用外部运行，导致安全评估结果（如攻击成功率0）实际上依赖云提供商过滤而非应用自身防护，这种依赖在切换后端时暴露无遗。

Method: ChannelGuard：一种无训练的深度防御框架。1) 在每个智能体间通道部署信息瓶颈门控；2) 通过嵌入相似度对通道文本与对抗性短语库进行评分；3) 根据评分决定放行、压缩或阻断；4) 不增加LLM调用开销；5) 使用归因方法记录防御层级。

Result: 1) 工具输出门控在三个不同后端（Azure GPT-5、Anthropic Sonnet 4.5、Haiku 4.5）上均100%阻断工具投毒攻击（30/30）；2) 提示注入攻击成功率从0.333降至0.167；3) GSM8K准确率保持不变（0.867）；4) 白盒自适应改写可绕过嵌入门控；5) 总评估成本仅47.36美元。

Conclusion: 多智能体LLM应用的安全评估必须报告跨后端的防御分布，而非仅报告最终攻击成功率。ChannelGuard提供了一种轻量级、跨后端一致的深度防御方案，但面临白盒自适应改写攻击的挑战。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM applications chain a planner, worker agents, a verifier, and a synthesizer, and every hop between agents is an unmonitored channel through which an adversary can smuggle instructions. Existing defenses guard only the input boundary (IBProtector, Llama Guard, perplexity filters, SmoothLLM) or run outside the application as opaque, stochastic provider-side filters. We show this gap carries a consequence rarely measured: on a 2,100-trace evaluation across eight attack families, five defenses, and three model backends, an undefended pipeline that appears fully safe under standard reporting (attack success 0.000 on tool- and memory-poisoning) owes that safety almost entirely to the cloud provider's server-side filter (54 of 60 blocks on Azure GPT-5), and silently shifts to the agent model's own alignment on a backend without such a filter. Outcome-only reporting hides this dependence. We present ChannelGuard, a training-free defense-in-depth framework placing information-bottleneck gates on every inter-agent channel; each scores channel text against an adversarial phrase bank by embedding similarity and deterministically passes, compresses, or blocks it, adding no LLM call, while an attribution method records which layer stopped each attack. ChannelGuard's tool-output gate blocks Tool Poisoning 30 of 30 at the application layer, identically across Azure GPT-5, Anthropic Sonnet 4.5, and Anthropic Haiku 4.5, whereas the undefended pipeline shifts entirely across backends; it also lowers Prompt Injection attack success by half (0.333 to 0.167) and preserves GSM8K accuracy exactly (0.867). White-box adaptive paraphrase evades every embedding gate, where a perturb-and-vote baseline does better. An extended appendix adds baselines, ablations, sweeps, a benign-preservation analysis, and a judge audit (kappa = 0.900), at a total cost of 47.36 USD.

</details>


### [125] [ChainWatch: A Kill Chain-Aligned Sequential Detection Framework for Multi-Step Attacks in MCP-Based AI Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19432)
*Om Narayan,Rashmi Jyoti,Ramkinker Singh*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出ChainWatch框架，利用六阶段杀伤链和隐马尔可夫模型检测MCP协议下AI代理系统中的多步工具调用攻击，能够识别传统单次防御无法发现的恶意序列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCP协议使AI代理能够连接外部工具和数据库，但攻击者可组合多个看似无害的工具调用形成恶意攻击链，现有逐次调用检测机制无法可靠识别此类多步攻击。

Method: 采用六阶段杀伤链建模攻击进程，结合隐马尔可夫模型对工具调用序列进行分类，构建20维特征提取方案捕获行为信号，并设计了直接序列攻击、间接提示注入链和混合多阶段攻击三类威胁模型。

Result: 在五个代表性攻击场景上验证，ChainWatch能够检测出传统逐次安全机制无法发现的攻击链。

Conclusion: ChainWatch为MCP-based AI代理系统提供了有效的多步攻击检测能力，填补了现有单次调用防御的空白。

Abstract: The Model Context Protocol (MCP) is an open-source standard that allows AI agents to connect to external tools, databases, and services. While this connectivity enables powerful agent capabilities, it also introduces multi-step attacks that existing per-call defenses cannot reliably detect. Attackers can compose individually benign tool invocations into malicious sequences that evade isolated inspection. This paper presents ChainWatch, a sequential detection framework for identifying multi-step attacks in MCP-based AI agent systems. ChainWatch models attack progression using a six-stage kill chain and applies a Hidden Markov Model (HMM) to classify tool-call sequences. Detection rules are triggered when a session exhibits suspicious progression across multiple stages. The framework is supported by a structured threat model covering direct sequential attacks, indirect prompt injection chains, and hybrid multi-stage attacks. A 20-dimensional feature extraction schema captures behavioral signals from tool interactions. We demonstrate the approach using five representative attack scenarios from the security literature, showing how ChainWatch detects attack chains that evade traditional per-call security mechanisms.

</details>


### [126] [Building Trust in Autonomous Commerce: A Verifiable Global Event Timeline and AI-Ready Fraud Intelligence Layer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19436)
*Rajat Srivastava*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体商业协议（如AP2、ACP）支持安全交易，但缺乏跨异构域的可互操作、防篡改审计能力及可验证时序排序，存在安全与信任缺口。

Method: 构建四个核心组件：规范事件模式（确定性序列化）、确定性批处理（无需同步时钟排序）、基于默克尔树的仅追加承诺（对数级包含证明）、区块链锚定（防篡改时间轴）。引入加密签名的欺诈标记和数据集血统模型。

Result: 默克尔树构建50,000事件耗时47毫秒；端到端验证低于0.013毫秒；包含证明从1,000事件的320字节对数增长至50,000事件的512字节；默克尔验证比线性扫描快14.4倍。

Conclusion: 提出的方案能高效实现跨域智能体商业的可验证审计、防篡改事件排序及可复现AI训练数据溯源，验证性能优异且扩展成本低。

Abstract: Agentic commerce protocols such as AP2 and ACP define mechanisms for secure agent-initiated transactions but do not provide interoperable, tamper-evident auditability or verifiable temporal ordering of events across heterogeneous domains. This paper addresses these gaps by proposing a verifiable global event timeline for agentic commerce, constructed from four core components: canonical event schemas that enforce deterministic serialization, deterministic batch formation ensuring reproducible ordering without reliance on synchronized clocks, Merkle-based append-only commitments providing logarithmic-cost inclusion proofs, and blockchain anchoring establishing a tamper-evident temporal backbone. Building on this infrastructure, we introduce a cryptographically signed fraud marker that binds risk labels to anchored evidence through an unforgeable provenance chain, and a dataset lineage model enabling reproducible, tamper-evident AI training pipelines. Empirical results from a prototype implementation demonstrate: Merkle tree construction processes 50,000 events in 47 milliseconds; end-to-end verification completes in under 0.013 milliseconds regardless of batch size; inclusion proof sizes grow logarithmically from 320 bytes at 1,000 events to 512 bytes at 50,000 events; and Merkle-based verification outperforms linear scan by 14.4x at 50,000 events.

</details>


### [127] [Intelligent Disruption: Undetectable Attacks on Wireless Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19448)
*Han Jiang,Jifa Zhang,Hu Jin,Nan Zhao,Mingqian Liu,Yunfei Chen*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 针对多对抗者场景下累积泄漏干扰(CLI)影响攻击隐蔽性的问题，本文提出了一种基于深度学习的智能攻击框架，通过深度神经网络功率控制降低干扰泄漏，并利用条件生成对抗攻击(CGAA)在动态环境中生成自适应扰动信号，仿真证明其在隐蔽性、攻击性和适应性上均优于基准方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多对抗者复杂场景中，多个并行攻击产生的累积泄漏干扰(CLI)增加了攻击被检测的风险，同时动态环境使得固定攻击策略难以保持稳定有效性，因此需要联合增强对抗攻击的隐蔽性、攻击性和适应性。

Method: 1) 基于深度神经网络的发射功率控制，通过调节多对抗者的发射功率来减少干扰泄漏，提升隐蔽性；2) 条件生成对抗攻击(CGAA)，以攻击信道信息为条件输入，生成器产生扰动信号使接收信号伪装成干净信号，判别器区分二者，通过对抗训练学习自适应扰动。

Result: 仿真结果表明，所提框架在攻击隐蔽性、攻击性和适应性方面均优于基准方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的深度学习智能攻击框架有效解决了多对抗者场景下CLI问题，在动态环境中实现了隐蔽、有效且自适应的对抗攻击。

Abstract: Adversarial attacks can degrade the legitimate decision performance in wireless autoencoder communications. However, in complex scenarios with multiple adversaries, the cumulative leakage interference (CLI) caused by the multiple parallel attacks increases the chance of detecting the attacks, while dynamical environments also make the fixed attack strategies difficult to have stable effectiveness. To jointly enhance the undetectability, aggressivity and adaptability of adversarial attacks, we propose a deep learning based intelligent attack framework. Specifically, considering the CLI caused by the multiple parallel attacks, a deep neural network based transmit power control is established to reduce the interference leakage by regulating the transmit power of these adversaries, thereby improving the undetectability. Furthermore, to enhance the attack effectiveness and stability in the dynamic environment, the conditional generative adversarial attack is further developed. The generator takes the attack channel information as the conditional input to produce the perturbating signals to mislead the discriminator by making the attacked received signals resemble the clean received signals, while the discriminator distinguishes between the two under the same condition. Through the adversarial training, the generator can learn to create adaptive perturbating signals with enhanced attack performance. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed framework outperforms benchmarks in terms of attack undetectability, aggressivity and adaptability.

</details>


### [128] [Integrity of peer-to-peer distributed LLM inference under malicious nodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19490)
*Mert Cihangiroglu,Antonino Nocera*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对去中心化LLM推理的完整性校验方法，通过混合预知正确激活值的“金丝雀”输入到正常流量中，利用激活值偏离程度检测恶意节点，无需固定阈值，实验达到AUROC 1.0。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在P2P分布式LLM推理中，各节点由不同方控制，任何节点都可能篡改输出破坏结果。现有方法（如已知答案陷阱、密码学承诺）仅检测精确正确性，无法容忍良性节点间的正常硬件噪声差异，缺少能区分恶意篡改与正常波动的完整性校验方法。

Method: 选择少量秘密的“金丝雀”输入，提前计算其正确激活值并混入正常查询流量中。由于节点无法区分金丝雀与真实请求，篡改节点也会污染金丝雀。通过测量实际激活值与已知参考的偏离程度，将良性节点硬件噪声导致的微小波动与恶意篡改导致的显著偏离区分开来，视为两个漂移分布的概率检验，不依赖固定阈值。

Result: 在408个配置（指标和成功标准在实验前固定）上，检测器达到AUROC 1.0，即在所有配置的所有金丝雀上，恶意分片的排名始终高于所有良性分片。

Conclusion: 该方法能有效检测去中心化LLM推理中的节点篡改行为，兼顾对良性硬件噪声的容忍与对恶意节点的精确识别。

Abstract: Peer-to-peer distributed inference executes a Large Language Model (LLM) on pooled consumer hardware by spreading its layers across many nodes. Every request passes through nodes that are owned and controlled by multiple independent parties. However, in this setting, any party can tamper with the output of its layers to corrupt the end result. Recomputing the forward pass on trusted hardware can catch this, but it introduces additional computational cost. The scientific literature includes several prior integrity-checking approaches, such as known-answer traps for image classifiers and cryptographic commitments. However, these solutions test only the exact correctness and do not account for the ordinary variation that may arise between benign nodes. In this paper, we propose a method that checks the output integrity by measuring the variation in the activations that each node passes to the next. A peer who wants to use the network selects a small set of secret canary inputs whose correct activations are known in advance and mixes them into regular traffic. Because the peers cannot tell a canary from a real query, any tampering node corrupts them as well. The deviation from the known reference then reveals malicious activity: benign nodes exhibit only minor variation from hardware-induced noise, whereas tampered nodes deviate far more. We treat the identification of malicious nodes as a probabilistic test that separates two drift distributions, without relying on a fixed threshold. We study 408 configurations with metrics and success criteria fixed before any experiment ran; the detector reaches AUROC 1.0, correctly ranking the malicious shard above every benign shard on every canary in every configuration.

*Zhanhao Hu,Dennis Jacob,Xiao Huang,Zhaorun Chen,Bo Li,David Wagner*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出Twin Agent双智能体架构，通过特权分离设计模式（Explore Agent处理不可信信息，Safe Agent执行特权操作）在保持任务效用的同时有效防御提示注入攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体易受提示注入攻击，而现有安全设计方案虽能缓解风险但往往降低任务效用且需要大量任务特定的工程工作。

Method: Twin Agent由两个近乎对称的智能体组成：Explore Agent负责检查不可信信息，Safe Agent负责执行特权操作。Explore Agent基于Safe Agent当前上下文进行条件化，仅向Safe Agent传输关于下一步行动的紧凑提示，从而在安全与效用之间取得更好平衡。

Result: 在SWE-bench Lite、AgentDojo和DecodingTrust-Agent三个基准测试上，Twin Agent在保持高任务效用的同时有效防御提示注入攻击，表现优于未防御的智能体和特权分离基线方法。

Conclusion: Twin Agent通过紧凑提示设计实现了更好的安全-效用权衡，是一种通用且有效的提示注入防御方案。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are vulnerable to security risks, such as prompt injection attacks from untrusted context that manipulate downstream reasoning and tool use. Existing secure-by-design approaches mitigate this risk by separating untrusted observations from privileged execution and careful control of information flow, but often degrade utility and require extensive task-specific engineering. We thus propose Twin Agent, a general privilege separation design pattern inspired by residual coding in the agent context. Twin Agent consists of two nearly symmetric agents: an Explore Agent that inspects untrusted information and a Safe Agent that executes privileged actions. The Explore Agent is conditioned on the Safe Agent's current context and communicates only compact hints to the Safe Agent about the next action to take. This design reduces the information needed to preserve task utility and thus achieves a better security--utility tradeoff, which we empirically verify by measuring how utility and attack success change as the length of hints varies. We evaluate Twin Agent on long-horizon software engineering tasks with SWE-bench Lite and on heterogeneous multi-tool interaction tasks with AgentDojo and DecodingTrust-Agent. Across both benchmarks, Twin Agent preserves high task utility while preventing prompt injection attacks, outperforming both undefended agents and privilege separation baselines.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出FedLSG框架：1）图与行为到文本的映射方案，将局部图结构和客户端更新行为转化为自然语言表示；2）轻量级师生架构，服务器端使用完整LLM作为教师进行全局上下文指导和恶意参与者检测，客户端使用LoRA学生进行语义推理以抑制后门触发器相关边的影响；3）将基于规则的信号自适应地融入消息传递和客户端聚合。

Abstract: Federated Graph Neural Networks (FedGNNs) are highly vulnerable to backdoor poisoning, yet existing defenses typically rely on rule-based approaches that lack semantic understanding, making them vulnerable to stealthy triggers and harmful to benign structures. To solve this, we present FedLSG, the first framework that integrates large language models (LLMs) into federated graph backdoor defense. FedLSG introduces a graph and behavior to text grounding scheme that transforms local graph structures and client update behaviors into semantically rich natural language representations. The framework further adopts a lightweight student-teacher architecture. On the server side, a full scale LLM serves as a teacher, providing global contextual guidance and evaluating client updates during aggregation to identify potentially malicious participants. On the client side, a LoRA-based student is maintained to perform semantic reasoning, to suppress the influence of edges associated with backdoor triggers. By enabling semantic interpretation of both graph patterns and client behaviors, the framework adaptively incorporates rule-based signals into message passing and client aggregation for defense. Experiments demonstrate that FedLSG significantly improves resistance to backdoor attacks without compromising graph integrity.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本攻击方法大多从语言模型中心迁移而来，优化时固定视觉输入，导致对抗提示词与特定图像绑定，跨图像迁移性差，限制了攻击效果。

Method: 提出GhostPrompt，采用联合优化策略，通过"最坏情况"生成方式蒸馏图像不变的对抗特征到提示词中，交替进行：为当前提示词构建困难视觉条件，以及更新提示词使其在这些条件下保持有效。

Result: 在主流VLM上，相比现有最优基线方法，攻击成功率提升超过30%，计算时间减少约70%。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are known to be vulnerable to adversarial attacks, where subtle perturbations to images or texts induce erroneous outputs. However, most text-based attacks are adapted from language-model-centric methods, in which the visual input is fixed during optimization, resulting in adversarial prompts that are tied to specific images and thus limiting their attack effectiveness. To this end, we first introduce a new research perspective: cross-image transferability for adversarial prompts. We then propose GhostPrompt, an adversarial prompt that is optimized once and reused to steer VLM outputs toward attacker-specified responses across diverse images. GhostPrompt employs a joint optimization that distills image-invariant adversarial features into the prompt by "worst-case" generation. Specifically, it alternates between constructing hard visual conditions for the current prompt and updating the prompt to remain effective under these conditions. Extensive experiments on prevalent VLMs verify that \ourmethod achieves an improvement of over 30% in attack success rates compared to state-of-the-art (SoTA) baselines, while reducing computation time by ~70%. Our code is avalable at https://github.com/Ye-ze-yu/GhostPrompt.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将每个攻击步骤建模为攻击单元（前提条件+攻击行为+后置条件），利用LLM多阶段流水线提取攻击行为骨架、恢复前提/后置条件、归一化为预定义谓词、修复断裂依赖，最后编译为Datalog规则进行攻击目标可达性推理。

Existing CTI extraction methods focus on indicators, entities, or TTP labels without modeling the execution conditions and resulting states of each attack step, so the extracted knowledge supports neither state matching nor reachability analysis across multi-stage attack chains. This paper proposes an automated framework that extracts reachable attack chains by modeling each attack step as an attack unit of preconditions, an attack behavior, and postconditions. A multi-stage pipeline assisted by large language models (LLMs) extracts attack behavior skeletons, recovers their preconditions and postconditions, normalizes them into predefined predicates, and repairs broken dependencies; the resulting units are compiled into Datalog-style rules for attack-goal reachability reasoning. On a dataset of 20 CTI reports containing 334 human-validated annotated steps, our framework achieves higher annotated-step coverage than representative CTI extraction systems in recovering attack behaviors. Moreover, by explicitly generating preconditions and postconditions, it produces attack units that are more complete and consistent than those generated by end-to-end LLM baselines. On the extracted chains, Datalog inference reaches the specified attack goal in 19 of 20 reports, while backward search yields 34 attack paths under the generated rules. The source code and experimental artifacts are available in an anonymized repository. .

### [135] [DARWIN: Evolving Jailbreak Adversary and Guardrail for LLM Safety Evaluation and Protection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19829)
*Weiwei Qi,Zefeng Wu,Zhilin Guo,Tianhang Zheng,Chaochao Lu,Liang He,Zhan Qin,Kui Ren*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出DARWIN框架，将越狱攻击视为开放式进化过程，通过持续攻防循环更新护栏。DARWIN-Attack通过策略发现、变异、选择和反馈驱动组合实现SOTA攻击效果；DARWIN-Guard通过在线对抗训练联合处理恶意和良性查询，提升鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM安全评估和防御方法采用静态范式，无法应对现实世界中不断进化的攻击者能力和持续扩展的攻击空间。

Method: 1) DARWIN-Attack: 进化式对抗方法，通过策略发现（外部来源）、变异（自我反思+遗传进化）、选择和反馈驱动组合，自适应选择策略进行攻击。2) DARWIN-Guard: 在线对抗训练范式，同时训练恶意和良性伪装查询，识别底层意图而非表面模式。

Result: 攻击端在多个前沿模型上实现SOTA，包括DeepSeek-V4-Pro和YuFeng-XGuard接近100%，GPT-5.5超90%成功率。防御端在12个安全基准上平均不安全召回率91.6%，优于YuFeng-XGuard和Nemotron Guard，同时在标准良性数据集上维持近100%通过率。

Conclusion: 动态进化攻防框架能有效应对持续演化的安全威胁，在线对抗训练可兼顾鲁棒性与实用性。

Abstract: Most existing LLM safety evaluation and defense methods follow a static formulation: jailbreak vulnerabilities are evaluated with fixed attack methods, and guardrails are trained on fixed malicious prompt datasets. However, real-world adversaries continuously evolve their capabilities and expand the attack space. To address this challenge, we propose DARWIN, an evolutionary attack-defense framework that formulates jailbreaking as an open-ended evolution process and continuously updates guardrails through an evolving attack-defense loop. DARWIN-Attack is an evolutionary adversary that expands its capabilities through strategy discovery, mutation, selection, and feedback-driven composition. It collects strategies from broad external sources, generates new variants through self-reflection and genetic evolution, and retains effective strategies based on their performance against aligned LLMs. During attack execution, DARWIN-Attack adaptively selects and combines evolved strategies according to feedback from target LLMs and guardrails. Across frontier models and guardrails, it achieves state-of-the-art attack success rates, including nearly 100% on DeepSeek-V4-Pro and YuFeng-XGuard and over 90% on GPT-5.5. On the defense side, we introduce DARWIN-Guard, an online adversarial training paradigm that iteratively learns from emerging adversarial samples generated by DARWIN-Attack. To improve robustness without sacrificing utility, DARWIN-Guard jointly trains on malicious and benign disguised queries, encouraging the model to identify underlying intent rather than superficial attack patterns. DARWIN-Guard achieves an average unsafe recall of 91.6% across 12 safety benchmarks, outperforming strong guardrails such as YuFeng-XGuard and Nemotron Guard, while maintaining a nearly 100% pass rate on standard benign datasets.

### [136] [Defense Against LLM Backdoors using Critical Neuron Isolation Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19894)
*Yuxi Li,Zhibo Zhang,Kailong Wang,Xingshuo Han,Ling Shi,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出DeCNIP方法，通过表征分析识别并剪除后门关键神经元，以统一流程防御LLM的后门攻击，在仅干预0.1%神经元的情况下实现95%以上的攻击成功率下降，并保持97%的正常性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有防御方法主要针对微调型后门，无法应对模型编辑攻击；且局限于分类任务，难以扩展到LLM的开放式生成场景；此外，这些方法依赖表面行为模式而忽视深层表征原因，缺乏机制性理解，导致鲁棒性、通用性和实用性不足。

Method: DeCNIP方法包含两个阶段：(1) 表征发现阶段，通过优化有害提示与候选token之间的交叉熵损失来识别触发行为，揭示后门劫持模型权重的潜在机制；(2) 后门关键神经元(BCNs)隔离与剪枝阶段，选择性地剪除恶意神经元以消除后门影响，同时保留模型正常功能。

Result: 在六个开源LLM和两个基准数据集上的实验表明，DeCNIP实现超过95%的攻击成功率相对降低，仅需0.1%的神经元干预，优于七种现有防御方法，并保持模型97%的正常性能。

Conclusion: DeCNIP通过机制性理解和表征分析，有效填补了现有防御方法在处理模型编辑攻击和开放式生成场景方面的空白，实现了高效、鲁棒且可扩展的LLM后门防御。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are vulnerable to backdoor attacks, where hidden triggers induce malicious outputs. Existing defenses generally fall into inference-time detection or training-time mitigation, but face two key limitations. First, they focus on fine-tuning-based backdoors (e.g., PEFT modules) and fail to address insidious model-editing attacks that bypass training pipelines. Second, they target simple classification settings and do not naturally extend to open-ended LLM generation and do not naturally extend to the open-ended generation characteristics of LLMs. Consequently, these methods focus on surface-level behavioral patterns while neglecting the deeper representational causes of malicious activations. This lack of mechanistic understanding forces defenses to depend on empirical heuristics, limiting their robustness, generality, and practical applicability in real-world LLM deployment.
  To bridge this gap, we introduce DeCNIP (Defense with Critical Neuron Isolation Pruning), which leverages representational analysis to identify and neutralize backdoors in a unified pipeline. Specifically, DeCNIP identifies trigger-like behaviors by optimizing a cross-entropy loss between harmful prompts with candidate tokens and benign inputs. This representational discovery exposes latent threats by uncovering mechanisms through which triggers hijack model weights. It then isolates Backdoor Critical Neurons (BCNs) and prunes them selectively to remove malicious influence while preserving model utility. Extensive evaluations on six open-source LLMs and two benchmark datasets demonstrate that DeCNIP achieves over 95% relative reduction in Attack Success Rate (ASR), outperforming seven state-of-the-art defenses with only 0.1% neuron intervention. Moreover, it maintains 97% of the model's performance on normal benchmarks, demonstrating its efficacy, robustness, and scalability.

</details>


### [137] [HijackKV: New Threat in Position-Independent KV Cache Reuse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19957)
*Yichi Zhang,Zhiqi Wang,Huan Zhang,Yuchen Yang*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文发现KV缓存重用机制存在安全漏洞，并提出首个攻击框架HIJACKKV，通过构造恶意前缀使良性文本的KV缓存编码攻击者意图，实现高达94%的单次攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KV缓存重用（如位置无关的缓存复用）虽能提升LLM推理效率，但仅通过token匹配检索缓存，忽略了KV中编码的上下文信息，导致安全风险。作者旨在揭示并系统性地利用这一漏洞。

Method: 提出HIJACKKV攻击框架，通过优化一个攻击者可控的前缀，使得后续常见良性文本计算出的KV缓存编码攻击者的目标，同时保持文本本身不变以确保缓存命中。

Result: 单次攻击平均成功率94%；在低命中率（10%）和频繁重计算（50%）等现实约束下仍有效；可在多轮交互中持续生效；支持黑盒跨模型迁移。

Conclusion: KV缓存重用机制存在严重安全隐患，需在设计安全的KV重用系统时考虑此类威胁；本文同时提供了防御设计思路。

Abstract: Key-Value (KV) cache reduces inference latency in large language models (LLMs). Traditional prefix-based reuse has low cache hit rates across inference requests because it requires exact token and position matches. To improve efficiency, recent system optimizations introduce position-independent KV reuse, allowing KV cache to be reused whenever identical text chunks appear, regardless of their position in the sequence.
  We show this design introduces a new threat, KV Cache Hijacking. Since KV caches are retrieved by token match but encode the context in which they were originally computed, the KV tied to a benign-looking token chunk may encode an attacker-controlled prefix. When later reused in a victim query, this contaminated KV silently hijacks the model's behavior, even if no attacker-controlled text appears in the input.
  We introduce HIJACKKV, the first attack framework that systematically exploits this vulnerability, demonstrating its severity and practicality. HIJACKKV optimizes an attacker-controlled prefix, so that the KV computed for a subsequent common benign text encodes the attacker's goal, while the text remains unchanged for future cache hits. HIJACKKV achieves an average 94% success rate in a single attempt, remains effective under realistic constraints including low hit rates (10%) and frequent recomputation (50%), persists over multi-turn interactions, and transfers across models in black-box settings. We further provide design insights for building secure KV reuse systems.

</details>


### [138] [Taming the Security-Energy Paradox: A Green AI Approach to Optimized Android Malware Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20003)
*Shrinidhi Sridhar,Vikas K. Malviya*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文研究了在Android设备上使用MLP模型进行恶意软件检测时，如何通过INT8量化技术平衡检测性能与能耗，发现量化后的浅层网络（3-4层）能在保持99.2%以上准确率的同时，将能耗降低至0.0189 mJ/次推理，模型体积缩小约3.5倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Android恶意软件日益增多，需要使用深度学习模型进行检测，但强检测模型会导致设备电池快速耗尽，存在安全性与能耗之间的权衡问题。

Method: 测试不同配置的多层感知机（MLP）模型，比较标准FP32模型与INT8量化神经网络在不同模型深度下的分类性能和能耗，使用TUANDROMD和DREBIN数据集进行评估。

Result: INT8量化使模型体积缩小约3.5倍，能耗降至0.0189 mJ/次推理，同时保持99.2%以上的检测准确率；浅层量化架构（3层和4层QNN）通过提高吞吐量、缩短CPU高功耗状态时间，进一步降低能耗。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，在资源受限的智能手机上可以实现高效的恶意软件防护，为移动安全领域的绿色AI奠定了基础。

Abstract: An increase in advanced Android malware requires the use of deep learning models, which can run on Android devices. But there is a trade-off between security and energy use, as strong detection models can drain the battery of devices fast. This work tests different Multi-Layer Perceptron (MLP) model configurations to balance malware detection performance and energy efficiency. In this work, we compared standard FP32 models with optimized INT8 quantized neural networks with different model depths using TUANDROMD and DREBIN datasets for both classification performance and energy consumption. The results show that INT8 quantization reduces model size by about 3.5 times with a decrease in energy consumption to 0.0189 mJ per inference, while maintaining more than 99.2\% detection accuracy. We found that shallow quantized architectures, such as 3-layer and 4-layer QNNs, reduce energy costs by improving throughput and shortening the time of CPU operating in a high-power state. This work shows that efficient malware protection can be achieved on resource-constrained smartphones and provides a foundation for Green AI in mobile security.

</details>


### [139] [Small, Free, and Effective: Orchestrating Open-Weight Small Language Models to Outperform Single LLM for Malware Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20216)
*Adel ElZemity,Shujun Li,Budi Arief*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文研究利用小型语言模型（SLM）的编排组合来替代大型语言模型（LLM）进行恶意软件分析。实验表明，混合编排架构（Qwen3-4B + Foundation-Sec-8B）在恶意软件报告分析中达到35.30%的准确率，超过了最强的网络安全专用基线（22.54%）和最强的无基础前沿模型基线（34.77%），证明基于证据的编排能显著提升协作SLM的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 恶意软件分析需要快速解析包含文件系统、网络和进程行为的复杂报告。虽然LLM在此领域表现优异，但闭源前沿模型存在不透明性和高昂API成本，而许多开源模型又因体积庞大、计算资源需求高而难以在资源受限环境中部署。因此，本文探索是否可以用编排组合的小型语言模型替代单个大型语言模型。

Method: 在Meta的CyberSecEval Malware Analysis基准上测试了11个开源SLM、3个网络安全预训练模型和6个前沿LLM建立基线。随后设计并评估了四种编排架构：(i)多智能体流水线，(ii)对抗性辩论框架，(iii)分层咨询系统，(iv)混合架构（证据驱动的流水线+对抗性辩论推理）。

Result: 混合系统（Qwen3-4B与Foundation-Sec-8B）整体准确率达35.30%，超过最强网络安全专用基线（22.54%）和最强无基础前沿基线（34.77%）；但使用相同证据流水线时，Gemini仍以38.22%保持最强配置。

Conclusion: 基于证据的编排可以显著提升协作SLM在恶意软件报告分析中的性能，为资源受限环境提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Malware analysis demands rapid interpretation of complex detonation reports spanning filesystem, network, and process behaviours. While large language models (LLMs) demonstrate impressive capabilities for technical artifact interpretation, the opacity and escalating API costs of closed-weight frontier models motivate exploration of open-weight alternatives. However, many open-weight models are large, demanding significant compute resources and incurring non-trivial hosting costs that place them beyond reach for resource-constrained deployments. This paper investigates whether orchestrated ensembles of small language models (SLMs) can match or exceed single LLM performance on structured questions about malware detonation reports. We established baselines by testing eleven open-weight SLMs, three cyber security pre-trained models, and six frontier LLMs on Meta's CyberSecEval Malware Analysis benchmark. We then designed and evaluated four orchestration architectures: (i) a multi-agent pipeline that decomposes analysis into structured evidence-collection and reasoning stages, (ii) an adversarial debate framework in which two agents iteratively critique each other's reasoning, (iii) a hierarchical consultation system that pairs a general-purpose SLM with a cyber-specialised expert model, and (iv) a hybrid architecture that combines evidence-grounded pipelines with adversarial debate reasoning. The hybrid system (Qwen3-4B with Foundation-Sec-8B) achieved 35.30% overall accuracy, exceeding the strongest cyber-specialised baseline (22.54%) and the strongest ungrounded frontier baseline (34.77%); when given the same evidence pipeline, grounded Gemini remained the strongest configuration at 38.22%. These findings show that evidence-grounded orchestration can substantially improve the performance of collaborative SLMs for supporting interpretation of malware detonation reports.

### [140] [The Ethics of Autonomous AI Agents for Offensive Security](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20255)
*Andreas Happe,Jürgen Cito,Jasmin Wachter*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文分析了LLM驱动的自主智能体在进攻性安全领域带来的三个核心不确定性维度（动作、影响、用户），指出这些特性与攻防成本不对称结合后，短期将有利于攻击者，并探讨了现有伦理框架的不足及利益相关者影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统渗透测试工具确定性强、范围窄且需要专业人员操作，而自主AI智能体带来了新的不确定性和安全挑战，现有框架无法应对这些变化，需要深入分析其伦理和实际影响。

Method: 从三个独立维度（非确定性策略、开放性影响、不确定用户群体）分析自主进攻性安全智能体的特性，结合攻防成本不对称理论，推演其对攻击者和防御者的短期与长期影响，并评估现有伦理框架的适用性。

Result: 发现自主安全智能体的三种不确定性与攻防成本不对称结合，短期内有利于攻击者并可能实现进攻能力的工业化；长期来看或能民主化防御实践；现有双用途网络安全和AI伦理框架无法有效应对这种组合。

Conclusion: 需要重新审视现有伦理框架，针对用户、工具制造者和第三方之间的道德归因模糊问题，提出分层建议以应对自主AI智能体在进攻性安全中带来的新挑战。

Abstract: LLM-driven autonomous agents are reshaping offensive security. Unlike traditional penetration-testing tooling -- deterministic, narrowly scoped, and operated by trained practitioners -- agentic security tools exhibit \textit{indeterminacy} along three independent dimensions. First, their actions are drawn from a non-deterministic policy whose outputs resist both ex-ante and ex-post explanation, frustrating incident attribution and pre-deployment safety review. Second, their impact is open-ended due to the non-deterministic actions, agency of utilized models, and opaque LLM supply-chains. Third, their user population is indeterminate in both size and required skill: the operating skill floor for using or developing offensive capabilities has dropped sharply. These three properties are linked thematically, but are not derivable from one another. Combined with the structural cost asymmetry between offense and defense, they enable the industrialization of offensive capability. The net short-term effect favors attackers, even if the same technology may, in the long run, democratize access to defensive practice. Existing dual-use cybersecurity and AI-ethics frameworks were not designed for this combination. Our work analyzes how moral attribution becomes diffuse between users, tool-makers, and third parties when employing autonomous AI agents for offensive security. We also examine the stakeholder impact of this technology and provide stratified recommendations.

### [141] [Chained Attacks on Drone-Based Federated Learning: From Network Disruption to Device Impersonation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20280)
*Suleiman Muhammad Sabo,Hamed Alkharsh,Peilin Li,Chuadhry Mujeeb Ahmed,Aydin Abadi,Shishir Nagaraja,Rajiv Ranjan*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文研究了针对无人机边缘智能系统中联邦学习（FL）的链式攻击，结合网络层拒绝服务（802.11去认证攻击）与凭证窃取后的身份冒充，并通过实验验证了该攻击在IID和Non-IID数据分布下对训练稳定性的破坏性影响，揭示了单因素认证的安全漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机联邦学习系统面临网络可用性与客户端认证双重安全威胁，现有研究缺乏对两者联合攻击（链式攻击）的系统性分析与量化评估。

Method: 通过系统文献综述与实证验证，在Raspberry Pi和Jetson两种测试平台上使用Flower框架，模拟802.11去认证攻击导致无人机离线，再利用提取的凭证冒充下线节点，分别在IID和Non-IID数据分布下评估攻击效果。

Result: 短期无线中断会导致训练严重不稳定，Non-IID条件下影响尤为显著；单因素认证无法阻止攻击者无缝替换断开节点。

Conclusion: 揭示了针对无人机FL系统链式攻击的严重威胁，指出需要同时解决可用性与认证漏洞，为未来防御策略提供了方向。

Abstract: Edge Intelligence (EI) has emerged as a transformative model for mission-critical unmanned platforms, such as drone swarms, by enabling collaborative model training at the network periphery. However, the security of FL deployments depends on both network availability and robust client authentication mechanisms. This paper investigates a chained attack against drone-based FL systems that combines network-layer denial-of-service with credential-based impersonation. We demonstrate that an adversary can: (1) force legitimate drones offline using 802.11 deauthentication attacks, and (2) subsequently impersonate the disconnected drone using extracted credentials. Through a systematic literature review and empirical validation using the Flower framework on two distinct testbeds of Raspberry Pi and Jetsons, we quantify the impact of availability disruptions under Independent and Identically Distributed (IID) and Non-Independently and Identically Distributed (Non-IID) data distributions, and confirm that single-factor authentication permits post-disconnect impersonation. Our findings reveal that even short-term wireless interruptions cascade into substantial training instability, particularly under non-IID conditions, while the authentication gap enables adversaries to seamlessly replace disconnected nodes. We discuss the compounded implications for mission-critical drone deployments and outline directions for future defenses addressing both availability and authentication vulnerabilities.

### [142] [Constant-time decoding of Gabidulin codes and their generalizations with application to RQC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20305)
*Nicolas Aragon,Chloé Baïsse,Anthony Fraga,Philippe Gaborit,Ilaria Zappatore*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文首次提出了增广Gabidulin码的恒定时间解码算法，实现了二次复杂度，并在RQC密码系统中验证了其性能与紧凑性之间的良好权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gabidulin码在基于秩的密码系统（如RQC、Loidreau）中应用广泛，但缺乏恒定时间实现，这对密码系统的实际安全部署至关重要。

Method: 提出了增广Gabidulin码的恒定时间解码算法，设计了q-多项式左除法的恒定时间算法，并完整描述了AG码的解码流程，集成到RQC-Block-MS-AG方案中。

Result: 实现了二次复杂度的恒定时间解码；性能优于原始RQC，比HQC慢约4倍，但密文和密钥尺寸约为HQC的1/4。

Conclusion: 该工作填补了Gabidulin码恒定时间实现的空白，在性能与紧凑性之间提供了有吸引力的权衡，适用于实际密码系统开发。

Abstract: Gabidulin codes are a rank metric analog of Reed-Solomon codes. Although these codes are used in different very efficient rank-based cryptosystems like the RQC cryptosystem or the Loidreau cryptosystem, there was no constant-time implementation of Gabidulin codes, when having a constant-time implementation is crucial for real-life development of cryptosystems. In this paper, we propose the first constant-time decoding algorithm of Augmented Gabidulin (AG) codes, a simple variation on Gabidulin codes where one adds zero columns to Gabidulin codes, and which contains the case of Gabidulin codes. These AG codes are used in practice in the most efficient variations of the RQC cryptosystem. We prove that AG code decoding can be achieved with quadratic complexity. We further present a constant-time algorithm for the left division of $q$-polynomials along with a complete description of the AG code decoding procedure. These algorithms are integrated into the RQC-Block-MS-AG scheme, and we evaluate the performance of our implementation through benchmarks. Our results show that our implementation outperforms the original RQC, though it remains approximately four times slower than HQC. However, it achieves ciphertexts and key sizes about four times smaller, highlighting an appealing trade-off between performance and compactness.

</details>

### [143] [Understanding Developer Pain Points in Federated Learning: Insights from Stack Overflow and GitHub](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19621)
*Sahand Saed,Khairul Alam,Banani Roy*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过对495个Stack Overflow帖子及92个FL相关项目的9,116个GitHub issues/PRs进行实证研究，系统分析了联邦学习开发者面临的主要挑战，识别出环境配置、API变更、非IID数据训练不稳定等九大Stack Overflow主题和十三大GitHub主题，并基于未解决率和中位解决时间评估了难点程度，最后为框架设计者、文档作者和教育者提供了改进建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习系统在构建和运维过程中存在分布式执行、框架快速演进以及隐私治理要求等困难，但目前缺乏对开发者实际面临挑战的系统性实证研究。本文旨在通过分析开发者社区的真实讨论数据，揭示FL开发中的主要痛点，为改善FL工具链和开发体验提供数据支撑。

Method: 收集495个Stack Overflow帖子及92个FL相关项目的9,116个GitHub issues/PRs，采用BERTopic主题建模进行主题提取，并利用未解决率、中位解决时间等难度指标对主题进行量化分析，同时按问题意图对帖子进行分类。

Result: 识别出Stack Overflow上9个主导主题和GitHub上13个主导主题，持续性的困难集中在环境设置与依赖兼容性、API断裂与迁移、非IID数据下的训练不稳定、评估与指标正确性、隐私保护机制集成等方面。其中"TFF安装与环境兼容性"和"联邦特征工程与SecureBoost问题"等主题表现出高未解决率和长解决时间。"How"类型的问题占比最高，反映开发者对程序性指导的强烈需求。

Conclusion: 研究结果为FL框架设计者、文档作者和教育者提供了可操作的改进建议。虽然结果局限于公开讨论和部分广泛使用的框架，但该研究提供了一种持续监控开发者痛点的可扩展方法，有助于提升FL系统的可用性、可靠性和可部署性。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative model training without centralizing raw data, but building and operating FL systems remains difficult due to distributed execution, rapidly evolving frameworks, and privacy and governance requirements. In this paper, we present an empirical study of FL developer challenges by independently analyzing 495 Stack Overflow posts and 9,116 GitHub issues and pull requests from 92 FL-related projects. Using BERTopic-based topic modeling and difficulty indicators such as unresolved rates and median resolution time, we characterize recurring problem areas and compare how they manifest across the two support platforms, Stack Overflow and GitHub. Our analysis surfaces nine dominant Stack Overflow topics and thirteen GitHub topics, with persistent difficulties concentrated in environment setup and dependency compatibility, API breakages and migration, training instability under non-IID data, evaluation and metric correctness, and the integration of privacy-preserving mechanisms. We also categorize posts by question intent to understand the kinds of help developers seek; this intent analysis shows that "How"-type questions dominate, reflecting strong demand for procedural guidance. Several topics, such as "TFF Installation and Environment Compatibility" and "Federated Feature Engineering and SecureBoost Issues," exhibit high unresolved rates and long resolution times, suggesting shortcomings in tooling, documentation, and debugging support. Based on these findings, we provide actionable implications for FL framework designers, documentation authors, and educators. Although our results are constrained to public discussions and a subset of widely discussed frameworks, the study offers a scalable method for continuously monitoring developer pain points and improving the usability, reliability, and deployability of FL systems.

</details>


### [144] [PerfAgent: Profiler-Guided Iterative Refinement for Repository-Level Code Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19653)
*Ryan Deng,Yuanzhe Liu,Bastian Lipka,Yao Ma,Xuhao Chen,Tim Kaler,Jatin Ganhotra*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: PerfAgent是一种基于性能分析器和验证器的闭环工作流，通过profiler引导和verifier反馈，显著提升LLM智能体在仓库级代码优化任务中的表现，将专家级优化补丁率从19.6%提升至39.2%（GSO）和从26%提升至74%（SWE-fficiency-Lite）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体在正确性导向的仓库级任务（如SWE-Bench问题修复）上表现良好，但在仓库级代码优化任务中表现不佳——优化需要保持行为不变的同时提升运行时性能，而现有智能体常忽略隐藏在抽象层和原生扩展后的性能瓶颈，仅做浅层优化，或未能充分测试导致破坏边界情况。

Method: PerfAgent采用profiler引导、verifier在环的工作流：1) 使用性能分析器（profiler）定位真实热点；2) 引入验证器（verifier）提供反馈，而非仅依赖运行时间判断；3) 支持超越首个通过补丁的持续改进，利用profiler证据而非简单计时决定下一步优化方向。

Result: 在GSO基准上，专家级别匹配补丁率从19.6%提升至39.2%；在SWE-fficiency-Lite上从26%提升至74%。此外，PerfAgent以更低成本超越了oracle best-of-five基线，证明性能提升来自更好的反馈机制而非额外的测试时采样。

Conclusion: 通过profiler引导和verifier反馈的循环机制，可以显著提升LLM智能体在仓库级代码优化任务上的能力，实现更高比例的专家级优化效果，且成本效益更优。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents now perform well on correctness-oriented repository-level tasks, including SWE-Bench issue resolution and feature implementation in real codebases. However, they still struggle with repository-level code optimization, which requires preserving behavior while improving runtime performance. Passing tests is not enough in this setting; a patch must preserve behavior, implement code optimization, and approach expert speedups. Current agents often miss bottlenecks hidden behind abstraction layers and native extensions, stop after shallow speedups, or insufficiently test the code patches that thus may silently break edge cases. We present PerfAgent, a profiler-guided, verifier-in-the-loop workflow that gives an off-the-shelf coding agent the feedback needed to find real hotspots, improve beyond the first passing patch, and use profiler evidence rather than timing alone to decide what to optimize next. On two challenging optimization benchmarks, GSO and SWE-fficiency-Lite, PerfAgent more than doubles the rate of expert-matching patches over OpenHands with GPT-5.1, improving from 19.6% to 39.2% on GSO and from 26% to 74% on SWE-fficiency-Lite. It also surpasses an oracle best-of-five baseline at substantially lower cost, showing that the gains come from better feedback rather than additional test-time sampling.

These experience-driven insights shaped CATGen's multi-stage design, which combines structured context retrieval, deterministic test skeleton construction, and program analysis-based post-processing. Current practices rely on unsustainable manual specifications, while LLM-based approaches suffer from hallucination and lack formal guarantees. To address this, we propose VeriSynth, a framework that synthesizes executable Python/Z3 verification models from Rust zkEVM code. ### [148] [Beyond Fail-to-Pass: Iterative Hardening of Co-Generated Bug Reproduction Tests and Fixes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19843)
*Yuhao Tan,Zhibang Yang,Fangkai Yang,Yuan Yao,Yu Kang,Lu Wang,Pu Zhao,Xin Zhang,Xiaoxing Ma,Qingwei Lin,Saravan Rajmohan,Dongmei Zhang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有BRT生成主要依赖fail-to-pass（F->P）标准评估，但该标准不足以衡量BRT对下游修复的实际帮助，存在宽松BRT虽满足F->P却仍允许错误补丁通过的问题。

Method: 提出CoHarden框架：1）将F->P BRT分为严格与宽松两类；2）利用宽松信号作为循环收敛标准；3）先生成测试再生成补丁；4）迭代强化测试与补丁对抗突变补丁，直至测试不再接受宽松回归。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have made automated program repair (APR) increasingly practical for real-world bugs, but repairing directly from bug reports remains underconstrained. Bug reproduction tests (BRTs) help close this gap by turning a bug report into an executable, bug-specific signal that can guide repair and validate candidate patches. Existing work has therefore studied BRT generation as a core subproblem in APR and mainly evaluates a generated BRT using the fail-to-pass (F->P) criterion, which requires the test to fail on the buggy code but pass on the golden fix. We show that F->P alone is insufficient when the goal of a BRT is to improve downstream repair. In particular, some F->P BRTs are lax, reproducing the observed symptom yet still admitting plausible-but-incorrect patches. We formalize this missing quality dimension by separating F->P BRTs into rigorous and lax ones, and show empirically that only the former consistently improve repair success. We further find that co-generation introduces test--fix error coupling, where the in-trajectory fail-to-pass (F->P) check can pass even when both the generated patch and generated test are wrong. Based on these findings, we propose CoHarden, a co-generation framework that uses the Lax signal as an in-loop convergence criterion. CoHarden first generates a test before any fix, then iteratively hardens the test and fix against surviving mutation patches until the generated test no longer admits Lax regressions. Experiments show that CoHarden reaches 69.4% Resolved and 78.9% F->P on SWE-bench Verified, outperforming the strongest fix-only and cogeneration baselines by +9.6 and +7.9 percentage points in Resolved, respectively, with consistent gains across LLM backbones and benchmarks.

On the other hand, existing LLMs often struggle to accurately capture the semantics of complex code, resulting in incorrect translations. To address these challenges, we propose a Translation fRAmework Via rule-guided reasoning and rEinforcement Learning, namely TRAVEL, consisting of two modules. The first module employs Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)-based reasoning path construction guided by Rust-specific rules, steering the search toward translation steps that respect the syntactic rules that LLMs frequently violate. The second module introduces reinforcement learning that couples execution feedback with reasoning-quality signals, encouraging the model to construct reasoning paths that accurately capture program semantics, thereby ensuring that the generated Rust code preserves the intended behavior of the original C program. We evaluate TRAVEL on three datasets: xCodeEval (a public benchmark), OS-Bench (functions collected from the Linux kernel), and HW-Bench (an industrial dataset from Huawei). Abstract: Fault injection is widely used to evaluate the resilience of microservice systems, where client requests often span multiple services and execution stages. Existing request-level techniques usually control where and what faults are injected, but not when they are activated within a distributed execution. This limitation makes it difficult to reproduce timing-dependent failures, such as failures after state-changing side effects, order-sensitive concurrent responses, and partial failures among repeated downstream calls. This paper presents SequenceFI, a non-intrusive framework for temporal fault injection in microservice systems. SequenceFI observes message-level send and receive events, propagates compact temporal evidence along request executions, and triggers faults only when occurrence-sensitive temporal guards are satisfied. It further synthesizes temporal guards from traces, reducing the need for exhaustive enumeration of temporal fault-injection configurations, while requiring no modifications to application code or serialization libraries. We implement SequenceFI on Kubernetes and evaluate it on four widely used microservice benchmarks. Across nine temporal-fault scenarios and 450 valid trials, SequenceFI achieves 100.0\% temporal success without premature or multiple injections, finds effective configurations in one attempt on average, and reduces aggregate end-to-end search time by 95.91\% compared with H-Random.

However, traditional CPDP methods suffer from the distribution shift between training and target projects that affects the model's performance. This paper proposes a novel CPDP framework that addresses this issue by proposing a two-stage multiple classifier system (MCS) selection scheme: one working at the project level and another at the module level. In the first stage, the framework evaluates multiple possible MCS configurations to find one that covers and generalizes well across multiple training projects. Consequently, the proposal is likely to obtain a diverse set of classifiers, each specialized in tackling software modules with distinct characteristics. The second selection stage operates at test time, selecting the most competent classifiers to predict each new module in the target project. Unlike previous approaches that apply the same classifiers to the entire target project, the proposed framework performs module-level model selection. This way, the system is more robust to changes in distributions between training and target projects because the selected set of classifiers is module-dependent. Our experimental results using 82 projects from four different CPDP benchmark datasets demonstrate that the proposed approach outperforms the state-of-the-art CPDP methods in most scenarios. The code, dataset, and further details about the proposed method are publicly available at https://github.com/jsaj/Multi_DES.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发者越来越多地通过提交序列化的相关变更而非单一大型变更来协调审查工作流。在Gerrit中，这些依赖关系形成关系链，但现有研究缺乏对关系链采用趋势及其对审查动态影响的系统量化分析。

Method: 分析了来自OpenStack、Wikimedia和ONAP三个Gerrit生态系统、15个仓库的29,580条关系链及401,256次变更。使用Mann-Kendall趋势检验、Mann-Whitney检验（含Cliff's delta效应量）进行链式与独立变更的对比，以及Spearman相关性分析基变更与衍生变更间的依赖关系。

Result: 关系链占比在项目间为5%-49%，14/15个项目呈增长趋势。链式变更合并时间中位数是同等规模独立变更的2.6倍，且差距随变更规模增大而扩大。审查活动在依赖链中显著协变（rho=0.43-0.61，14-15/15个项目），33.5%的链成员在审查期间经历结构演化。

Conclusion: 关系链作为持久的、受生态系统塑造的协调单元运作，具有内部结构，这是仅关注单一变更的分析无法捕捉的。未来的审查分析、审阅者分配系统和AI辅助审查工具应基于关系链而非孤立变更进行推理。

Abstract: Background. Developers increasingly coordinate dependent review workflows by submitting sequences of related changes rather than monolithic ones. In Gerrit, these dependencies form relation chains: structured review units that link changes together. As chains become more common, they shape review activities through synchronization overhead, CI amplification, and merge-ordering constraints.
  Aim. We investigate how developers adopt relation chains and how these dependency structures influence review dynamics and outcomes.
  Method. We analyze 29,580 relation chains from 15 repositories across three Gerrit ecosystems (OpenStack, Wikimedia, and ONAP), comprising 401,256 changes, using Mann-Kendall trend tests, Mann-Whitney tests with Cliff's delta for chain-vs-solo comparisons, and Spearman correlations for base-descendant dependencies.
  Results. Chain prevalence ranges from 5% to 49% across projects, increasing in 14 of 15. Chain changes take a median of 2.6 times longer to merge than size-matched solo changes, with the gap widening for very large changes. Review effort propagates through dependency-linked review workflows: base-change review activity co-varies with descendant review activity (rho = 0.43-0.61 in 14-15 of 15 projects), and 33.5% of chain members undergo structural evolution during review.
  Conclusions. Relation chains operate as durable, ecosystem-shaped coordination units with internal structure that change-centric analyses cannot capture. Future review analytics, reviewer-assignment systems, and AI-assisted review tools should reason over chains rather than isolated changes.

</details>


### [153] [Don't Trust the Label: License Laundering in AI Supply Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20300)
*James Jewitt,Hao Li,Gopi Krishnan Rajbahadur,Bram Adams,Ahmed E. Hassan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究追踪了23万余条数据集→模型→应用链，发现62.3%的链条中存在无许可证声明的人工制品，且具有义务的许可证类别在端到端传播中的存活率均低于7%，而宽松许可证存活率达95.1%，揭示了AI供应链中的许可证洗钱问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管AI制品在跨平台供应链中流动时许可证义务应随 redistribution 传播，但目前尚无研究衡量这些义务是否在链条中得以保留或被剥离替换。

Method: 追踪232,270条数据集→模型→应用链，量化两种许可证洗钱形式：无声明制品在下游获得明确标签，以及声明类别在 redistribution 中被替换。

Result: 62.3%的链条经过至少一个无许可证声明的制品；所有义务性许可证类别端到端存活率低于7%，而宽松类别达95.1%。

Conclusion: 为从业者、模型发布者、权利人和平台所有者提供了可操作的建议。

Abstract: AI artifacts move through a multi-platform supply chain, spanning datasets and models on Hugging Face and applications on GitHub. While each artifact carries a license whose obligations should propagate through redistribution, no study has yet measured whether those obligations survive the chain or are stripped and replaced as artifacts move downstream. We trace 232,270 dataset$\rightarrow$model$\rightarrow$application chains and quantify two forms of license laundering: when artifacts with no declared license acquire definitive labels downstream, and when one declared license category replaces another during redistribution. We find that 62.3% of chains pass through at least one artifact with no declared license (concentrated in a small set of foundational datasets), and that every obligation-bearing license category falls below 7% end-to-end survival while the Permissive category reaches 95.1%. Based on these findings, we provide actionable recommendations for practitioners, model publishers, rights holders, and platform owners.

</details>


### [154] [Multi-Source and Cross-Scenario Strategy-Guided Code Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20353)
*Yuwei Zhao,Qianyu Xiao,Ye Cui,Yijun Yu,Yingfei Xiong*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出MoST框架，通过跨知识源和跨场景的策略整合与迁移，显著提升LLM代码优化的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有策略引导的代码优化方法只能利用历史提交中的策略，无法利用教科书、网页等其他知识源，且策略只能应用于原始场景，无法跨场景迁移。

Method: MoST将不同知识源的信息统一表示为证据对象，通过自平衡加权聚类算法进行跨源跨场景聚类以识别策略，并通过示例迁移过程将策略迁移到目标场景以生成静态分析规则。

Result: 在151个C/C++、150个Python和50个Rust优化任务上，相比SemOpt，MoST的精确匹配补丁和语义等价补丁分别提升24.44%-180.00%和21.88%-37.50%。在15个真实项目中，最大性能提升19.72%-717.42%，平均提升4.44%-258.17%。

Conclusion: MoST通过融合多源跨场景策略有效提升了LLM代码优化的性能，显著优于现有方法。

Abstract: Automated code optimization improves program performance by refactoring source code, and recent studies use LLMs to generate optimization patches. The newest approaches are strategy-guided: they summarize strategies from historical optimization commits as static analysis rules, and use these rules to match code locations for LLMs to optimize. However, these approaches have two limitations: (1) the strategies may come from other knowledge sources, such as textbooks and web pages, but the existing approaches cannot utilize them; (2) a strategy may be applicable to different scenarios, e.g., different programming languages, but existing approaches can only formalize strategies for the scenario to which the source commit belongs. To address these limitations, we propose MoST, an LLM-based code optimization framework that integrates multiple knowledge sources across scenarios. MoST uniformly represents items in different knowledge sources as evidence objects, clusters them in a cross-source and cross-scenario manner to identify strategies, and transfers them to the target scenario when necessary for generating static analysis rules. To implement this process, MoST employs a novel self-balanced weighted clustering algorithm to balance evidence objects from different knowledge sources, and a novel example transfer procedure to ensure the quality of the generated rules when transferring across scenarios. On a benchmark containing 151 C/C++, 150 Python, and 50 Rust historical optimization tasks, compared with SemOpt, MoST yields 24.44%-180.00% and 21.88%-37.50% more patches that are exactly the same as or semantically equivalent to developer patches, respectively. When optimizing 15 real-world projects, MoST achieves 19.72%-717.42% maximum improvements and 4.44%-258.17% average improvements for the performance tests in the projects, significantly outperforming SemOpt and Codex.

</details>


### [155] [The ICSE 2026 Shadow PC: Training the Next Generation of Reviewers Through Deliberate Practice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20396)
*Christian Kästner,Michael Hilton,Jonathan Bell,Francisco Gomes de Oliveira Neto*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文介绍了ICSE 2026 Shadow PC项目，通过多阶段结构、校准和同伴反馈等创新设计，实现了大规模审稿人培训。102名参与者完成了117篇论文的评审，97%推荐该体验，67%的作者认为评审有帮助，展示了严格审稿培训的可扩展性。

Method: 重新设计的Shadow PC项目，包含多阶段结构（校准+同伴反馈）、与主PC严格分离、以及领导力发展路径。

Result: 102人完成项目并评审117篇论文；97%参与者推荐该体验；67%作者认为评审有帮助。

Abstract: Peer review is essential to software engineering research, yet reviewer training remains largely implicit.
